> ## ⚠ UNVERIFIED / HEURISTIC — read this first
> These tag→hook links are **inferred from source structure, not confirmed.**

>   file. Fairly strong, but "appears in the same file" ≠ "is this hook."
> - **same-subsystem**: a hook in the same Ext family as the parse site. A wide net.
> The one thing here that IS confirmed is the **parse site** (where the tag is read).
> Vanilla (non-framework) tags are out of scope — see Phase D (Ghidra).
